        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;

        }

        }

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

Steps to reproduce the problem:



<b class="line"><!---->Steps to reproduce the problem:<!----></b>



<br>





1. Run the following Python server that will send an invalid result and then on the next request send a download.



<span class="line"><!---->1. Run the following Python server that will send an invalid result and then on the next request send a download.<!----></span>



<br>





from http.server import BaseHTTPRequestHandler, HTTPServer



<span class="line"><!---->from http.server import BaseHTTPRequestHandler, HTTPServer<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





sessions = set()



<span class="line"><!---->sessions = set()<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):



<span class="line"><!---->class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):<!----></span>



<br>





    def do_GET(self):



<span class="line"><!---->    def do_GET(self):<!----></span>



<br>





        if (self.path not in sessions):



<span class="line"><!---->        if (self.path not in sessions):<!----></span>



<br>





            self.send_response(200)



<span class="line"><!---->            self.send_response(200)<!----></span>



<br>





            self.send_header("Cache-Control", "no-store")



<span class="line"><!---->            self.send_header("Cache-Control", "no-store")<!----></span>



<br>





            message = "<invalid>"



<span class="line"><!---->            message = "&lt;invalid&gt;"<!----></span>



<br>





            self.wfile.write(bytes(message, "utf8"))



<span class="line"><!---->            self.wfile.write(bytes(message, "utf8"))<!----></span>



<br>





            self.end_headers()



<span class="line"><!---->            self.end_headers()<!----></span>



<br>





            sessions.add(self.path)



<span class="line"><!---->            sessions.add(self.path)<!----></span>



<br>





        else:



<span class="line"><!---->        else:<!----></span>



<br>





            self.send_response(200)



<span class="line"><!---->            self.send_response(200)<!----></span>



<br>





            self.send_header('Cache-Control', 'no-store')



<span class="line"><!---->            self.send_header('Cache-Control', 'no-store')<!----></span>



<br>





            self.send_header('Content-Disposition','attachment;filename="file.txt"')



<span class="line"><!---->            self.send_header('Content-Disposition','attachment;filename="file.txt"')<!----></span>



<br>





            self.end_headers()



<span class="line"><!---->            self.end_headers()<!----></span>



<br>





            message = "file contents"



<span class="line"><!---->            message = "file contents"<!----></span>



<br>





            self.wfile.write(bytes(message, "utf8"))



<span class="line"><!---->            self.wfile.write(bytes(message, "utf8"))<!----></span>



<br>





            sessions.remove(self.path)



<span class="line"><!---->            sessions.remove(self.path)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





with HTTPServer(('', 8000), handler) as server:



<span class="line"><!---->with HTTPServer(('', 8000), handler) as server:<!----></span>



<br>





    server.serve_forever()



<span class="line"><!---->    server.serve_forever()<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





2. Create a sand-boxed iframe with allow-popups



<span class="line"><!---->2. Create a sand-boxed iframe with allow-popups<!----></span>



<br>





let f = document.createElement('iframe');



<span class="line"><!---->let f = document.createElement('iframe');<!----></span>



<br>





f.sandbox = 'allow-popups';



<span class="line"><!---->f.sandbox = 'allow-popups';<!----></span>



<br>





f.srcdoc = '<a target="_blank" href="



<span class="line"><!---->f.srcdoc = '&lt;a target="_blank" href="<!----></span>





http://localhost:8000">Click



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="http://localhost:8000&quot;>Click"><!---->http://localhost:8000"&gt;Click<!----></a>





 me</a>';



<span class="line"><!----> me&lt;/a&gt;';<!----></span>



<br>





document.body.appendChild(f);



<span class="line"><!---->document.body.appendChild(f);<!----></span>



<br>



<br>



<br>





3. Click the thing that says click me and wait.



<span class="line"><!---->3. Click the thing that says click me and wait.<!----></span>



<br>





It should open a popup to an error page that then reloads automatically to the download.



<span class="line"><!---->It should open a popup to an error page that then reloads automatically to the download.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Problem Description:



<b class="line"><!---->Problem Description:<!----></b>



<br>





A page reload automatic or otherwise before a popup has finished loading for the first time results in bypassing the download protection of a sandboxed page.



<span class="line"><!---->A page reload automatic or otherwise before a popup has finished loading for the first time results in bypassing the download protection of a sandboxed page.<!----></span>



<br>





(Shows new URL but still in old sites process at least no padlock)



<span class="line"><!---->(Shows new URL but still in old sites process at least no padlock)<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->Kinda related: <!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->Issue 1339639<!----></span>

class handler(BaseHTTPRequestHandler):

    def do_GET(self):

        if (self.path not in sessions):

            self.send_response(200)

<span class="line"><!---->            self.send_header('Cross-Origin-Opener-Policy', 'same-origin')<!----></span>

            message = "<invalid>"



<span class="line"><!---->            message = "&lt;invalid&gt;"<!----></span>

            self.wfile.write(bytes(message, "utf8"))



<span class="line"><!---->            self.wfile.write(bytes(message, "utf8"))<!----></span>

            self.end_headers()



<span class="line"><!---->            self.end_headers()<!----></span>

            sessions.add(self.path)



<span class="line"><!---->            sessions.add(self.path)<!----></span>

<br>



<br>





The NavigationDownloadPolicy is currently computed by the renderer



<span class="line"><!---->The NavigationDownloadPolicy is currently computed by the renderer<!----></span>



<br>





process. The problem: not every navigation is initiated from the



<span class="line"><!---->process. The problem: not every navigation is initiated from the<!----></span>



<br>





renderer. This is a problem.



<span class="line"><!---->renderer. This is a problem.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Most fields from the bitfield can also be computed from the browser



<span class="line"><!---->Most fields from the bitfield can also be computed from the browser<!----></span>



<br>





process. This patch computes the one related to the 'allow-download'



<span class="line"><!---->process. This patch computes the one related to the 'allow-download'<!----></span>



<br>





sandbox flags from the navigation request. In the future, I believe we



<span class="line"><!---->sandbox flags from the navigation request. In the future, I believe we<!----></span>



<br>





want to do something similar for the other properties.



<span class="line"><!---->want to do something similar for the other properties.<!----></span>

Fixes for low severity bugs do not get backmerged, however reviewing this issue and the fix, this issue seems to be sufficiently more serious than originally expected and triaged. Adjusting severity to medium and keeping issue in merge review queue. 



<span class="line"><!---->Fixes for low severity bugs do not get backmerged, however reviewing this issue and the fix, this issue seems to be sufficiently more serious than originally expected and triaged. Adjusting severity to medium and keeping issue in merge review queue. <!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Just a quick note in ref to comments #13 and #15, security severity is not part of the VRP process. While VRP may adjust severity based on assessment and analysis, severity assignment (or adjustment) should very much occur before VRP as it drives triage, prioritization, and security merge review processes as well. Please always feel free to reach out if a severity reassessment is needed from security or we can help answer any questions about severity or other outcomes of security triage. Thanks!



<span class="line"><!---->Just a quick note in ref to comments #13 and #15, security severity is not part of the VRP process. While VRP may adjust severity based on assessment and analysis, severity assignment (or adjustment) should very much occur before VRP as it drives triage, prioritization, and security merge review processes as well. Please always feel free to reach out if a severity reassessment is needed from security or we can help answer any questions about severity or other outcomes of security triage. Thanks!<!----></span>

ctrl/middle/contextual-menu navigation initiated by the the user are intentionally not considered to be part of it. They should behave 'as-if' the user copy and pasted the URL into a new tab.



<span class="line"><!---->ctrl/middle/contextual-menu navigation initiated by the the user are intentionally not considered to be part of it. They should behave 'as-if' the user copy and pasted the URL into a new tab.<!----></span>



<br>

> Just a quick note in ref to comments #13 and #15, security severity is not part of the VRP process. While VRP may adjust severity based on assessment and analysis, severity assignment (or adjustment) should very much occur before VRP as it drives triage, prioritization, and security merge review processes as well. Please always feel free to reach out if a severity reassessment is needed from security or we can help answer any questions about severity or other outcomes of security triage. Thanks!



<span class="line"><!---->&gt; Just a quick note in ref to comments #13 and #15, security severity is not part of the VRP process. While VRP may adjust severity based on assessment and analysis, severity assignment (or adjustment) should very much occur before VRP as it drives triage, prioritization, and security merge review processes as well. Please always feel free to reach out if a severity reassessment is needed from security or we can help answer any questions about severity or other outcomes of security triage. Thanks!<!----></span>



<br>

[M109] Fix NavigationDownloadPolicy from the browser process



<span class="line"><!---->[M109] Fix NavigationDownloadPolicy from the browser process<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





The NavigationDownloadPolicy is currently computed by the renderer



<span class="line"><!---->The NavigationDownloadPolicy is currently computed by the renderer<!----></span>



<br>





process. The problem: not every navigation is initiated from the



<span class="line"><!---->process. The problem: not every navigation is initiated from the<!----></span>



<br>





renderer. This is a problem.



<span class="line"><!---->renderer. This is a problem.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





Most fields from the bitfield can also be computed from the browser



<span class="line"><!---->Most fields from the bitfield can also be computed from the browser<!----></span>



<br>





process. This patch computes the one related to the 'allow-download'



<span class="line"><!---->process. This patch computes the one related to the 'allow-download'<!----></span>



<br>





sandbox flags from the navigation request. In the future, I believe we



<span class="line"><!---->sandbox flags from the navigation request. In the future, I believe we<!----></span>



<br>





want to do something similar for the other properties.



<span class="line"><!---->want to do something similar for the other properties.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>

<span class="line"><!---->(cherry picked from commit <!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.

        }

      </style>
